{\n    \"useDocOrientationClassify\": False,\n    \"useDocUnwarping\": False,\n    \"useChartRecognition\": False,\n}\n\n# 忽略环境变量里的 HTTP(S)_PROXY，避免失效/不适用的系统代理导致 ProxyError\n_http = requests.Session()\n_http.trust_env = False\n\n\ndef build_chunk_pdf_bytes(src_doc: fitz.Document, start: int, end: int) -> bytes:\n    \"\"\"Extract pages [start, end) (0-based, end exclusive) into a PDF byte string.\"\"\"\n    new_doc = fitz.open()\n    try:\n        new_doc.insert_pdf(src_doc, from_page=start, to_page=end - 1)\n        buf = io.BytesIO()\n        new_doc.save(buf)\n           return False, f\"响应非 JSON: {e}\", None\n        if \"result\" not in body:\n            return False, f\"响应缺少 result: {str(body)[:400]}\", None\n        return True, None,   output_dir: str,\n    chunk_idx: int,\n    page_from: int,\n    page_to: int,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Write markdown and images for one API response under a per-chunk folder.\"\"\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    layout_results = result[\"layoutParsingResults\"]\n    for i, res in enumerate(\n        tqdm(layout_results, desc=f\"  保存 chunk {chunk_idx} (页 {page_from + 1}-{page_to})\", leave=False)\n    ):\n        md_filename = os.path.join(output_dir, f\"doc_{i}.md\")\n        with open(md_filename, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as md_file:\n            md_file.write(res[\"markdown\"][\"text\"])\n\n        for img_path, img_url in tqdm(\n            res[\"markdown\"][\"images\"].items(),\n            desc=f\"    md 图 doc_{i}\",\n            leave=False,\n        ):\n            full_img_path = os.path.join(output_dir, img_path)\n            os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(full_img_path) or \".\", exist_ok=True)\n            img_bytes = _http.get(img_url, timeout=120).content\n            with open(full_img_path, \"wb\") as img_file:\n                img_file.write(img_bytes)\n\n        for img_name, img_url in tqdm(\n            res[\"outputImages\"].items(),\n            desc=f\"    版面图 doc_{i}\",\n            leave=False,\n        ):\n            img_response = _http.get(img_url, timeout=120)\n            if f.write(img_response.content)\n            else:\n                print(f\"Failed to download image {img_name}, status: {img_response.status_code}\")\n\n\ndef main() -> None:\n    output_root = \"output\"\n    os.makedirs(output_root, exist_ok=True)\n\n    src = fitz.open(file_path)\n    try:\n        total_pages = src.page_count\n        chunk_ranges = [\n            (s, min(s + PAGES_PER_CHUNK, total_pages))\n            for s in range(0, total_pages, PAGES_PER_CHUNK)\n        ]\n        desc = f\"PDF 分片 (每档 {PAGES_PER_CHUNK} 页) → API\"\n        for chunk_idx, (start, end) in enumerate(tqdm(chunk_ranges, desc=desc, unit=\"档\")):\n            chunk_bytes = build_chunk_pdf_bytes(src, start, end)\n            file_data = base64.b64encode(chunk_bytes).decode(\"ascii\")\n            payload = {\n                \"file\": file_data,\n                \"fileType\": 0,\n                **optional_payload,\n            }\n\n            last_err: str | None = None\n            result: dict | None = None\n            max_attempts = 1 + API_RETRY_TIMES\n\n            for attempt in range(max_attempts):\n                ok, err, res = _post_layout_parse(payload)\n                if ok and res is not None:\n                    result = res\n                    break\n                last_err = err or \"unknown\"\n                if attempt >= max_attempts - 1:\n                    break\n                # 4xx（除 429）一般重试无意义，直接结束本档\n                if err and err.startswith(\"HTTP \"):\n                    parts = err.split(None, 2)\n                    try:\n                        code = int(parts[1].rstrip(\":\")) if len(parts) > 1 else 0\n                    except ValueError:\n                        code = 0\n                    if 400 <= code < 500 and code != 429:\n                        break\n                delay = RETRY_DELAY_BASE_SEC * (2**attempt)\n                time.sleep(delay)\n\n            if result is None:\n                print(\n                    f\"\\n[跳过] chunk {chunk_idx} 页 {start + 1}-{end}，已重试仍失败: {last_err}\"\n                )\n                fail_note = os.path.join(\n                    output_root,\n                    f\"FAILED_chunk_{chunk_idx:03d}_p{start + 1:05d}-{end:05d}.txt\",\n                )\n                with open(fail_note, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n                    f.write(last_err or \"\")\n                continue\n\n            chunk_dir = os.path.join(output_root, f\"chunk_{chunk_idx:03d}_p{start + 1:05d}-{end:05d}\")\n            save_chunk_results(result, chunk_dir,         codeText: "# uv run python merge_markdown.py\n# 将 output/chunk_* 下 doc_*.md 按顺序拼接为一个文件；仅改写图片 src 路径，不插入其它文字。\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport argparse\nimport os\nimport re\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom tqdm import tqdm\n\nCHUNK_DIR_RE = re.compile(r\"^chunk_(\\d+)_p(\\d+)-(\\d+)$\")\nDOC_FILE_RE = re.compile(r\"^doc_(\\d+)\\.md$\")\n\n\ndef parse_chunk_dirs(output_root: Path) -> list[tuple[int, Path]]:\n    \"\"\"返回 (chunk_idx, 路径)，按 chunk_idx 排序。\"\"\"\n    rows: list[tuple[int, Path]] = []\n    for p in output_root.iterdir():\n        if not p.is_dir():\n            continue\n        m = CHUNK_DIR_RE.match(p.name)\n        if m:\n            rows.append((int(m.group(1)), p))\n    rows.sort(key=lambda x: x[0])\n    return rows\n\n\ndef list_doc_files(chunk_dir: Path) -> list[Path]:\n    found: list[tuple[int, Path]] = []\n    for p in chunk_dir.glob(\"doc_*.md\"):\n        m = DOC_FILE_RE.match(p.name)\n        if m:\n            found.append((int(m.group(1)), p))\n    found.sort(key=lambda x: x[0])\n    return [p for _, p in found]\n\n\ndef rewrite_image_paths(md_text: str, chunk_dir: Path, merged_out: Path) -> str:\n    \"\"\"按合并文件所在目录，把 src=\\\"imgs/...\\\" 改为指向该分片目录下的 imgs/。\"\"\"\n    base = merged_out.parent.resolve()\n    chunk_resolved = chunk_dir.resolve()\n    prefix = Path(os.path.relpath(chunk_resolved, base)).as_posix()\n\n    def sub(m: re.Match[str]) -> str:\n        q = m.group(1)\n        return f\"src={q}{prefix}/imgs/\"\n\n    return re.sub(r'src=([\"\\'])(\\./)?imgs/', sub, md_text)\n\n\ndef starts_with_atx_heading(text: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"片段首部（允许前导空白）是否为 Markdown ATX 标题，如 ## 、 ### 等。\"\"\"\n    return bool(re.match(r\"\\s*#{1,6}\\s\", text))\n\n\ndef main() -> None:\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description=\"合并 output/chunk_* 下的 Markdown\")\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"-i\",\n        \"--input-dir\",\n        type=Path,\n        default=Path(\"output\"),\n        help=\"paddle 输出目录（默认 ./output）\",\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"-o\",\n        \"--output\",\n        type=Path,\n        default=Path(\"output\") / \"merged_full.md\",\n        help=\"合并后的文件路径（默认 ./output/merged_full.md）\",\n    )\n    args = parser.parse_args()\n\n    output_root = args.input_dir.resolve()\n    out_path = args.output.resolve()\n\n    if not output_root.is_dir():\n        raise SystemExit(f\"输入目录不存在: {output_root}\")\n\n    chunk_rows = parse_chunk_dirs(output_root)\n    if not chunk_rows:\n        raise SystemExit(f\"未找到 chunk_* 子目录: {output_root}\")\n\n    out_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    out_path_resolved = out_path\n\n    parts: list[str] = []\n\n    for _idx, chunk_path in tqdm(chunk_rows, desc=\"合并分片\", unit=\"档\"):\n        for doc_path in list_doc_files(chunk_path):\n            text = doc_path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n            text = rewrite_image_paths(text, chunk_path, out_path_resolved)\n            if parts and starts_with_atx_heading(text) and not parts[-1].endswith(\"\\n\"):\n                parts.append(\"\\n\\n\")\n            parts.append(text)\n\n    out_path.write_text(\"\".join(parts), encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    print(f\"已写入: {out_path}（{len(chunk_rows)} 个分片目录）\")\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",

                      children: "却说艳冰欲谨和说出当年之百忍，谨和以早岁丑事，说恐见笑；皇甫尚以佳不丑，迫令说之。谨和只得言之曰：“老朽先住在山下官道旁，与贱内年各不惑，未生男女，贫无生业，唯卖豆腐度日。一日，风雪霏霏，户掩柴扉，路断人迹。薄暮见一老叟，敝衣跣足，张破伞冒雪而过，怜而呼入。以壶酒与御寒。叟感之，知老朽贫未生子，于怀中取出一张字赠之，曰：‘此乃太和图，上有一百忍字，请勉而行之。若行一忍，圜去一字，至完满，财、子、寿随之矣。’言讫留不住，仍冒雪而去，不言姓氏，衣虽褴褛，气色不俗，形迹甚异。因不敢疏忽，遂将百忍图贴内厅壁上。数日霜雪始霁，拮据本钱开店。清早豆腐正捧出架，适遇两狗相咬，豆腐架却被撞倒，豆腐尽覆于地，一狗之足被架伤跛而散。须臾，跛狗之主来较曰，掷伤他狗将毙，索偿寻殴。老朽不敢与较，即将身上衣服脱偿之，以温语褒去。随进内厅，将忍字圜去一个。次日又贷本开市，有一孩童，父与二文钱来买豆腐，孩童匿去一文买饼吃了，只一文买豆腐。老朽打一文豆腐与之端回去，其父兄赶来，以欺骗小童，二文钱只与一文钱货，将豆腐一起翻倒。老朽只是认错，赔尽不是，送还二文钱方歇。赶收店门进去，又圜去一忍字。那时无处再借本开店，因"

    })
  }) : _createMdxContent(props);
}

  default: MDXContent
